A lot of people are saying this isn't a rip off of Among Us, but they have the same exact mechanics with a few small differences. It's not like this is just a mode based on the murder mystery idea, it's literally based on among us.  Every murder mystery type game has different rules, mafia has everyone sitting in a circle with the mafia killing people and everyone trying to guess who it is. Werewolf has cards and stuff. TTT has guns and running around, Gmod murder mystery has an investigator.   But the mechanics of this and Among Us are almost identical. They have the same exact terms, votes, ejections, etc. The imposter isn't even really an imposter, they are more so a traitor. It's so obvious they are just copying Among Us to gain popularity.
